     <p> Coniferous trees shroud the trail, snowy boughs creaking beneath the weight of their wintery burden. A single post marks a fork in the ancient road, the signage weathered beyond legibility. </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('oAuiciSa');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> The chopped head of a Troll was left to rot near the base of the tallest mountain.   </p>  <h5> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('I6RcRRPd');"><i class="fa (or <a class="btn-spawn-dice" data-dice='1d6' onclick="javascript:window.app.spawn_dice('1d6');"><strong>2 in 6</strong></a> chance if camping overnight) to be ambushed or preyed upon by: </p>  <table bludgeoning, piercing and slashing from nonmagical attacks</li>   <li><strong>Senses: </strong> blindsight 120 ft.</li>    </ul>  <hr/> <div><ul> <li><strong>Legendary Resistance (3/Day):</strong> If the tarrasque fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.</li><li><strong>Magic Resistance:</strong> The tarrasque has advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.</li><li><strong>Reflective Carapace:</strong> Any time the tarrasque is targeted by a TAG:spell spell, a line spell, or a spell that requires a ranged attack roll, roll a <a class="btn-spawn-dice" data-dice='d6' onclick="javascript:window.app.spawn_dice('d6');"><strong>d6</strong></a>. onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('bAVqSC4c');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> The burned remains of a small village can be found on the edge of the cliffs, at the end of a winding steep trail.
